\DoxyCodeLine{01583\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ cl\_uint\ getVersion(\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ *versionInfo)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01584\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ highVersion\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01585\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ lowVersion\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01586\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ index\ =\ 7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01587\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}\ (versionInfo[index]\ !=\ \textcolor{charliteral}{'.'})\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{01589\ \ \ \ \ highVersion\ +=\ versionInfo[index]\ -\/\ \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{01590\ \ \ \ \ ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01591\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01592\ \ \ ++index;}

\DoxyCodeLine{01594\ \ \ \ \ lowVersion\ *=\ 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01595\ \ \ \ \ lowVersion\ +=\ versionInfo[index]\ -\/\ \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{01596\ \ \ \ \ ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01597\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01598\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ (highVersion\ <<\ 16)\ |\ lowVersion;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01599\ \}}
